  PRIMARY KEY (`access_filter_rule_id`),
  KEY `FK_access_filter_rule_chain` (`access_filter_chain_id`),

  `picture_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `device_id` int NOT NULL,
  `picture_name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `time_stamp` datetime NOT NULL,
  `track_data_id` bigint DEFAULT NULL,
  `camera_id` smallint NOT NULL,
  `total_packets` smallint NOT NULL,
  `last_packet` smallint DEFAULT NULL,
  `completed` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `picture_bytes` mediumblob,
  `thumbnail_bytes` mediumblob,
  `new` tinyint DEFAULT NULL,
  `rotation` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` int NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`picture_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UC_picture_device_picture` (`device_id`,`picture_name`),
  KEY `FK_picture_track_data_id` (`track_data_id`),
  KEY `FK_camera_picture_user_id` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_camera_picture_user_id` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_picture_track_data_id` FOREIGN KEY (`track_data_id`) REFERENCES `track_data` (`track_data_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE

-- Table structure for table `default_poi_location`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `default_poi_location`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!50503 SET character_set_client = utf8mb4 */;
CREATE TABLE `default_poi_location` (
  `location_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `custom_id` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NOT NULL,
  `application_id` int NOT NULL,
  `longitude` double NOT NULL,
  `latitude` double NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` varchar(128) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin DEFAULT NULL,
  `hilbertid` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `location_category_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `last_modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `custom_fields` json DEFAULT NULL,
  `cf_facet` text CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_general_ci GENERATED ALWAYS AS (concat(coalesce(json_unquote(json_extract(`custom_fields`,_utf8mb4'$[*].v')),_utf8mb4''),_utf8mb4' ',coalesce(`name`,_utf8mb4''),_utf8mb4' ',coalesce(`description`,_utf8mb4''))) STORED,
  PRIMARY KEY (`location_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UK_default_poi_location_location_category_id_custom_id` (`custom_id`,`location_category_id`),
  KEY `IX_default_poi_location_category_hid` (`location_category_id`,`hilbertid`),
  FULLTEXT KEY `cf_facet` (`cf_facet`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_default_poi_location_category` FOREIGN KEY (`location_category_id`) REFERENCES `default_poi_location_category` (`location_category_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=59361 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_bin;

  `last_modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`location_category_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `custom_id` (`custom_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UC_location_cat_app_name` (`application_id`,`name`),

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `device`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!50503 SET character_set_client = utf8mb4 */;
CREATE TABLE `device` (
  `device_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `device_name` varchar(64) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bo_type` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `owner_id` int NOT NULL,
  `hide_position` int DEFAULT '0',
  `proximity` double DEFAULT '0',
  `IMEI` varchar(36) DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone_number` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_ip` varchar(64) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_port` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `static_ip` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `static_port` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `longitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `latitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `ground_speed` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `altitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `heading` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_stamp` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `milliseconds` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `protocol_id` varchar(16) DEFAULT NULL,
  `protocol_version_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `valid` smallint DEFAULT '1',
  `apn` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gprs_username` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `gprs_password` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `dev_def_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `msg_field_dict_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `mobile_network_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `outgoing_transport` varchar(16) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_password` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_settings_profile_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `device_username` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `transport_protocol` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`device_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Index_email` (`email`),
  KEY `FK_user_id_2` (`owner_id`),
  KEY `FK_device__dev_def_id` (`dev_def_id`),
  KEY `FK_device_msg_field_dict` (`msg_field_dict_id`),
  KEY `FK_device_mobile_network` (`mobile_network_id`),
  KEY `Index_imei` (`IMEI`),
  KEY `index_device_phone` (`phone_number`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_device__dev_def_id` FOREIGN KEY (`dev_def_id`) REFERENCES `device_def` (`dev_def_id`) ON DELETE SET NULL ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_device_mobile_network` FOREIGN KEY (`mobile_network_id`) REFERENCES `mobile_network` (`mobile_network_id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_device_msg_field_dict` FOREIGN KEY (`msg_field_dict_id`) REFERENCES `msg_field_dictionary` (`msg_field_dict_id`) ON DELETE SET NULL ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_user_id_2` FOREIGN KEY (`owner_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=26598 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

  KEY `Inx_rule` (`expression_evaluator_id`),

CREATE TABLE `geofence` (
  `geofence_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `geofence_name` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `geofence_description` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `application_id` int NOT NULL,
  `min_longitude` double NOT NULL,
  `max_longitude` double NOT NULL,
  `min_latitude` double NOT NULL,
  `max_latitude` double NOT NULL,
  `min_altitude` double NOT NULL,
  `max_altitude` double NOT NULL,
  `bo_type` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`geofence_id`),
  KEY `FK_geofence_application` (`application_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_geofence_application` FOREIGN KEY (`application_id`) REFERENCES `applications` (`application_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `location`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;

CREATE TABLE `location` (
  `location_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `lon` double NOT NULL,
  `lat` double NOT NULL,
  `country_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `city_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `postal_code_number` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_number` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_box` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `address` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `administrative_area_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `sub_administrative_area_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `point_of_interest` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `location_category_id` int unsigned NOT NULL,
  `hid` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `revision` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`location_id`),
  KEY `IDX_position` (`lon`,`lat`,`location_category_id`),
  KEY `IDX_point_of_interest` (`point_of_interest`,`description`,`location_category_id`),
  KEY `IDX_hid` (`location_category_id`,`hid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_location_category` FOREIGN KEY (`location_category_id`) REFERENCES `location_category` (`location_category_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=41851 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

  `name` varchar(45) NOT NULL,
  `description` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `category` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `managable` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `tags` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bo_reader_assembly_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `bo_reader_type_name` varchar(128) DEFAULT NULL,
  `kind` tinyint NOT NULL,
  `app_local_objs` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`privilege_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Index_privilege_name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=239 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

--
-- Table structure for table `provider_message`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `provider_message`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!50503 SET character_set_client = utf8mb4 */;
CREATE TABLE `provider_message` (
  `provider_message_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `client_device_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `client_user_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `sender_user_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `client_address` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `message` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `queue_id` int NOT NULL,
  `delivery_status` int NOT NULL,
  `outgoing` tinyint NOT NULL,
  `timestamp_client` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `timestamp_queued` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `timestamp_delivered` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `timestamp_last_try` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `retry_count` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `transport` varchar(16) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`provider_message_id`),
  KEY `FK_provider_message_client_device_id` (`client_device_id`),
  KEY `INX_provider_message_client_user_id` (`client_user_id`),
  KEY `INX_provider_message_sender_user_id` (`sender_user_id`),
  KEY `INX_provider_message_queue_id` (`queue_id`),
  KEY `INX_provider_message_delivery_status` (`delivery_status`),
  KEY `Index_provider_message_timestamp_client` (`timestamp_client`),
  KEY `IDX_transport_outgoing_timestamp` (`transport`,`outgoing`,`timestamp_queued`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_provider_message_client_user_id` FOREIGN KEY (`client_user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_provider_message_queue_id` FOREIGN KEY (`queue_id`) REFERENCES `provider_message_queue` (`provider_message_queue_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_provider_message_sender_user_id` FOREIGN KEY (`sender_user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=57256 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

  `hash` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `job_label` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,

  `rendering_time` int DEFAULT NULL,

  `time_stamp_last_process_started` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_stamp_first_render_started` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_stamp_last_render_started` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `time_stamp_error` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `cmd_queue_item_id` bigint DEFAULT NULL,
  `file_ids` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ondemand_process_log_id`),
  KEY `Inx_hash` (`hash`,`steps`,`steps_executed`),

  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `report_definition_id` int NOT NULL,
  `renderer_id` int NOT NULL,
  `application_id` int NOT NULL,
  `show_parameters` int NOT NULL,

  CONSTRAINT `FK_reportv3_report_renderer` FOREIGN KEY (`renderer_id`) REFERENCES `reportv3_renderer` (`report_renderer_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_reportv3_report_report_definition` FOREIGN KEY (`report_definition_id`) REFERENCES `reportv3_report_definition` (`report_definition_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE

  `report_id` int NOT NULL,

  `last_update_time` datetime NOT NULL,
  `scheduled_time` datetime NOT NULL,
  `period_start` datetime DEFAULT NULL,

  `report_error_message` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,

  PRIMARY KEY (`scheduled_report_status_id`),
  KEY `INDEX_report_status_times` (`scheduled_time`,`last_update_time`),

  KEY `IDX_scheduled_report_times` (`scheduled_for`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_report_state_report_id` FOREIGN KEY (`report_id`) REFERENCES `reportv3_report` (`report_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_scheduled_report_status_ondemand_process_log_id` FOREIGN KEY (`ondemand_process_log_id`) REFERENCES `reportv3_ondemand_process_log` (`ondemand_process_log_id`) ON DELETE SET NULL ON UPDATE CASCADE

CREATE TABLE `schoolbus_activity` (
  `date` date NOT NULL,
  `bus_id` int NOT NULL,
  `student_id` int NOT NULL,
  `time` varchar(8) NOT NULL,
  `login_lat` decimal(10,7) NOT NULL,
  `login_lon` decimal(10,7) NOT NULL,
  `logout_lat` decimal(10,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  `logout_lon` decimal(10,7) DEFAULT NULL,
  `logout_type` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `logout_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `violation` tinyint NOT NULL,
  `login_address` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `logout_address` varchar(500) DEFAULT NULL,
  `has_address` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`date`,`bus_id`,`student_id`,`time`),
  KEY `fk_schoolbus_activity_bus_id_idx` (`bus_id`),
  KEY `fk_schoolbus_activity_student_id_idx` (`student_id`),
  KEY `fk_schoolbus_has_address_idx` (`has_address`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_schoolbus_activity_bus_id` FOREIGN KEY (`bus_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_schoolbus_activity_student_id` FOREIGN KEY (`student_id`) REFERENCES `schoolbus_student` (`schoolbus_student_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='Junction table between schoolbus_student and users';

  `max_longitude` double DEFAULT NULL,

  `dirty_count` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `parent_track_info_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `parent_owner_id` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `dirty_time_stamp` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `start_latitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `start_longitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_latitude` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `end_longitude` double DEFAULT NULL,

  KEY `FK_track_category_1` (`track_category_id`),
  KEY `Index_dirty_check` (`dirty_time_stamp`),
  KEY `Index_parent_track_info` (`parent_track_info_id`),
  KEY `Inx_ti_owner_min_time` (`owner_id`,`min_time_stamp`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_track_category_1` FOREIGN KEY (`track_category_id`) REFERENCES `track_category` (`track_category_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `FK_user_2` FOREIGN KEY (`owner_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`user_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE

/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!50503 SET character_set_client = utf8mb4 */;
CREATE TABLE `web_service_script` (
  `web_service_script_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `application_id` int NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `script` text NOT NULL,
  `enabled` tinyint NOT NULL,
  `script_app_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`web_service_script_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UC_web_service_script_app_name` (`application_id`,`name`),
  KEY `FK_web_service_script_script_app_id` (`script_app_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_web_service_script_app` FOREIGN KEY (`application_id`) REFERENCES `applications` (`application_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `web_service_script_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`script_app_id`) REFERENCES `script_app` (`script_app_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3;

CREATE TABLE `workspace` (
  `workspace_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int NOT NULL,
  `application_id` int NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(90) NOT NULL,
  `state` mediumtext NOT NULL,
  `shared` int NOT NULL,
  `created` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`workspace_id`),
  KEY `FK_workspace_application` (`application_id`),
  KEY `FK_workspace_user` (`user_id`),
